Took my car in for a quick 15 minute smog around 1630.  While waiting i went across the street to the DMV.  Came back and was told my car failed due to my catalyst system wasn't ready.  They recommended to drive 100 or 200 miles then come back. I was still told i would have to pay $42 just for failing smog.  It would cost me another $25 for retest plus certificate on my next visit.  I was eager for a retest so i decided to take my car down the street to Nice & Easy smog.  I was greeted by a kind older lady with a friendly smile. <response>None< /response><Review>Overall, Anchor did an excellent job repairing my vehicle in a prompt manner once I finally dropped it off. From a customer service perspective, however, they dropped the ball multiple times, and I was very disappointed with them, and I would not go back unless I am able to communicate more clearly with the repair shop.

Anchor is apparently a Mercury-approved repair facility. I was in a rear-end accident which did not require significant work, with no structural damage, and only largely cosmetic damage to my rear bumper. I'd already worked things out with Mercury, who'd accepted liability for the accident, and recommended this shop. I called the shop, who told me to come out, which I did.

They did a quick estimate, and told me that they'd reach out to Mercury to confirm that it was okay to fix my car. I asked if I should leave the car there. They said no. I thought this was odd, but they said that I should't leave my car until Mercury confirmed. This being the end of the day on a Monday, they said they'd email me my estimate tonight (they failed to do that) submit it to Mercury and get back to me the next day (they also failed to do that). So I went back to work, thinking I'd just wasted a lot of time driving out, getting the car looked at, and accomplishing nothing, then going back to work. Mercury happens to call me asking why I haven't dropped off the car. I told them that the shop told me not to, and Mercury says the shop should not have told me that. I'm peeved.

After not hearing anything all day Tuesday, the shop calls me back on Wednesday and let me know Mercury will pay for it after all. I need to go back and drop off the car now. We set up an appointment for Monday.

On the next Monday, I call to say I'm going to drop off the car. They can't seem to remember me for a while, but then discover they haven't ordered parts. I'm glad they told me, otherwise I'd have wasted another trip over there. We set up another appointment for the following Monday.

Finally, the next Monday, I drop off the car, two weeks after the initial estimate. By now I'm rather upset, as this is the third time I've blocked off time on my calendar to go to this shop. I fill out some forms, and they say they'll email with progress. I get zero updates, and finally a voicemail where they say they're finishing up my car a few days later. I can't tell if they're finished from the voicemail, so I have to call them again to confirm it's actually done, not just almost done. Finally, I go pick it up. At least they washed the exterior and vacuumed the interior, though they didn't do a great job, since I have bird poop streaks on my hood still. Guess I'll need another wash.

Long review, mediocre experience. I didn't give fewer stars because the actual car-fixing is what is most important, and that was done rather well. I guess that's something.</Review></record>

Luna Grill is awesome if you eat out everyday and are looking for a healthy yet satisfying change up. I think the targeted diner is someone who doesn't cook often themselves and wants something healthy. The food is mild and light and tasted neutral and fresh.

The dining room is also nice and clean with ample lighting. This is more of a lunch place and there is a steady stream of people. It was pleasant to sit and eat here. It takes about 10 minutes to get your order.

The sticking point though is the food is good but not great. It's pretty standard and for that I have a hard time giving it more than 3 stars. It was A-OK. The quantity was average. You can get the same quality food in a lot of other places and this place just doesn't stand out enough to garner another star.<//Text>

< Text>
Came in for a quick bite before heading out to a women's volleyball game at UCI.  Place is super clean and very organized.  Staff is very pleasant and courteous.  Food is great and generous portions.

My wife ordered chicken kabab plate that was excellent. Large pieces of chicken breast seasoned perfectly, the salad is fresh and crispy with a hint of citrus, rice was scrumptious. I ended up ordering a cheeseburger (again) with fries (frites, basically).  Just how fries are supposed to be, crispy and brown on the outside and soft on the inside with just the perfect amount of salt.

Food takes a bit of time, but I'm assuming because the food here is made to order? At least it seems that way.  Oh, a BIG PLUS, beer and wine is served here!<//Text>

What a find!! I have been missing PizzaRev which closed it's Santa Barbara location last year, due to pre existing management issued quadrupled by the pandemic.

Tried blaze for the first time today due to a pie day offer.  Make your own pizza for $3.14.

I like my pizza loaded with everything - combination of spicy red and pesto sauce, mozerella, gorgonzola, feta, goat cheese,  chicken, olives, bell peppers, onions, spinach, red peppers, jalapeno, basil, roasted garlic topped with pesto butter. Well done to handle the weight of all these toppings.

It tasted great!</text>

< Text>
You choose your toppings as you move down the line, and the counter person puts them on your pizza as you go. There's no limit to the number of toppings; the build your own pizza option comes at a single low price, regardless of how many toppings you choose.  (I don't really see the advantage of the predesigned "signature" pizzas.) The pizza comes in only one size, but you can order half a pizza if you want. The crust is amazingly thin, and comes out delightfully crisp. All in all, this is one of the best pizzas around.<//Text>

< text>
Been here a few times and haven't been disappointed. So I decided to do this review. Customer service is great. Had menudo a few ago and have to say it's pretty good. They serve it con grano ( with hominy) and I prefer without. The lady gladly said she will remove it and they did. Ordered a side of queso fresco to go with my tortillas. Delicious. Most recently we went and my wife ordered camarones a la diabla and I had a torta of lengua. The camarones were irresistible and had to pinch a couple off my wife's plate. The sauce had its kick so you better like spicy to try these.  The torta was good. Love the toasted bouillon and the lengua was just melting in my mouth. Not like other places I've tried where they left the skin from the tongue. This is a good place to bring your family.</text>

< review>
This place has some good solid Mexican food but the service is disappointing. Be aware when you walk in there you're supposed to seat yourself and wait for a waiter...that I didn't know. I was standing awkwardly there for like 10 mins and nobody even bothered to greet me. When I finally figured it out the waitress took another 10 mins to get to me. Mind you I speak Spanish and asked several times for assistance.

The food is good. They give you big portions it just takes a while to come out. I spent around an hour and a half here just literally waiting most of the time. By the way when you come here, you go straight up to the counter to pay, they never come around to give you a check (wish I got the memo).

I think this is a one time place to go, there's so many other Mexican spots around. If you want to kill time here's the place to go!<//review>
